=========== Extracted Query =============
Select o_orderkey as orderkey, Max(c_acctbal) as revenue, o_orderdate as orderdate, o_shippriority as shippriority
From customer, orders, lineitem
Where c_custkey = o_custkey and o_orderkey = l_orderkey and c_mktsegment  = 'BUILDING' and o_orderdate  <= '1995-03-13' and l_shipdate  >= '1995-03-17'
Group By o_orderkey, o_shippriority
Order By revenue desc, orderdate asc
Limit 10;
